    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer4527811292453213967">As the captain of a schooner catering to the elite on the Caribbean Seas, Sebastian Stark does his best to avoid any human encounters.   <span id="freeText4527811292453213967" style="display:none">As the captain of a schooner catering to the elite on the Caribbean Seas, Sebastian Stark does his best to avoid any human encounters. Interacting with people isn’t his thing, and he prefers the company of a bottle of vodka, a shot glass, and maybe a whore. There’s no doubt he’s hiding from a checkered past, but he does well keeping everything to himself…<br /><br />…until the night his schooner capsizes, and he’s stuck on a life raft with one of the passengers.<br /><br />Raine’s young, she’s cute, and Bastian would probably be into her if he wasn’t suffering from alcohol withdrawal. As the days pass, DTs, starvation, and dehydration become the norm. Even the most closed person starts to open up when he thinks he’s going to die, but when she realizes their traumatic pasts are connected, it’s no longer the elements that have Bastian concerned.<br /><br />He has no idea how he’s going to Survive Raine.</span>

<div id="review_599440311" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/599440311" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/599440311?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599440311" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16016991039880237802"><b>♥ 5 STARS. ♥</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Your body can survive in amazing situations; you just have to convince your mind to do what you tell it to do."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418983ra/830095.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418983i/830096.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>What. A. Story.</b> <br/><br/><i>Surviving Raine</i> was an <b>amazing, heartfelt, emotional, gripping and unforgettable story</b> that simply blew me away. For the day and a half it took me to read this book, it completely consumed my thoughts. And even now, after having finished it, I often still think about it. Yes, that's just how good this book was. <br/><br/><b>Surviving Raine</b> is a story about tw</p></span>
  <span id="freeText16016991039880237802" style="display:none"><b>♥ 5 STARS. ♥</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Your body can survive in amazing situations; you just have to convince your mind to do what you tell it to do."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418983ra/830095.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418983i/830096.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What. A. Story.</b> <br><br><i>Surviving Raine</i> was an <b>amazing, heartfelt, emotional, gripping and unforgettable story</b> that simply blew me away. For the day and a half it took me to read this book, it completely consumed my thoughts. And even now, after having finished it, I often still think about it. Yes, that's just how good this book was. <br><br><b>Surviving Raine</b> is a story about two people having to survive together on a tiny life raft after their ship has capsized. They have to suffer through all the harsh conditions that come with surviving a shipwreck: starvation, dehydration, infections... but the toughest aspect to survive might not be the physical conditions, but the emotional journey both survivors have to go through. <br><br><br><b>Sebastian Stark --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794237i/589194._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Sebastian {Bastian} Stark</b> is the captain of <i>The Oblivion</i>, a ship that sails it's passengers on their vacation throughout the Caribbean Seas.<br><br>Bastian is rude, crude, crass and the perfect epitome of <i>badass</i>. <br><br>He's not a people's person, not at all. He much prefers the company of a pack of cigarettes, a bottle of vodka and a whore every now and then.<br><br>He's used to caring about no one but himself, but when his ship capsizes and he is stuck on a life raft with one of his female passengers, his sense of responsibility kicks in and he becomes quickly aware that from now on his safety isn't the only one he needs to care about anymore.<br><br><b><i>"For once, it wasn't just me I needed to look after. There was the annoying, questioning, tiny little piece of seriously feminine, soft, brown-eyed, doesn't-take-my-shit, fucking beautiful young woman who didn't stand a chance on her own that I needed to protect."</i></b><br><br>At first, Bastian and Raine don't get along very well. They argue, a lot. Bastian suffers from alcohol withdrawal and since there's no else to take it out on, Raine is often the victim of one of his outrages outbursts...<br><br><i><b>"Well, is there something I can do to help with that?" she asked, "or are you just going to yell at me all the time?"</b><br><br>That was it. I couldn't hold my temper back any longer.<br><br><b>"Yeah, there is something you can do," I said coldly, turning my glare at her. "Come here and blow me. That would probably ease a bit of my tension - especially if you swallow."</b><br><br>Yeah, I know. I couldn't believe I said it either."</i><br><br>Well, at least, Bastian knew what an ass he could be at times and I have to admit, despite him being mean and cruel in the beginning, after a while he grew on me. I liked his direct approach of things and the fact that, despite his hard exterior, deep down he's actually a nice person with a big hart; he just doesn't know how to show it.<br><br><br>And then there's sweet, innocent <b>Raine Gayle</b>...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418983i/830097.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's pretty much the complete opposite of Bastian; she's caring, compassionate and just downright a good person. Everything Bastian is not. <br><br>Still, she finds herself drawn to him and when both of them start opening up about their past, they start to grow closer to each other.<br><br>And you know, two people spending days alone with each other, thinking that they might never make it out of their messed up situation alive, that's bound to create some sexual tension. (and trust me, there were some serious HOT and sexy scenes between the two of them!).<br><br><i><b>"I could do it, you know," I heard myself say. My voice had dropped low, but I knew she still heard me. I leaned over only a little, bringing my mouth closer to her ear. "I could make you come without touching you."</b></i><br><br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418983ra/830098.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But despite the fact that they start to grow more comfortable around each other, Bastian finds it hard to let himself be vulnerable around Raine. His past makes it hard for him to trust anyone other than himself and he's afraid that if he opens himself up to her, he'll never be able to <i>survive Raine</i> if he ever were to lose her...<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Please stop shutting me out."<br>... <br>"I never let you in, baby."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418983i/830099.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want to, Raine," I said quietly. "I want to let you in. I just don't know if I can."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Bastian is such an interesting character and I loved that the entire story was written in his point of view. He's made a lot of mistakes in his life but it was touching to see how being with Raine changed him and how it made him want to be a better person.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418983i/830100._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luckily, the story ends with an implied HEA, but the very last chapter does give the impression that Raine and Bastian's adventure isn't over yet and that there might even be a follow up to the story...<br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br> <br><i>"So long as men can breathe, or eyes can see,<br>So long lives this, and this gives life to thee."<br><br><br><b>"I give you my life, my love, my soul,"</b> I swore to her. <b>"As long as I'm breathing, I'm yours. Even when I'm nothing more than a fucked up dick, I still love you."</b></i> <br><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418983ra/830101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Shay Savage</b> has written a unique, captivating and intriguing story that will stay with me for a very long time and that I would highly recommend everyone to read. <b>Surviving Raine</b> is the first story I've read by her and I already know it won't be my last!<br><br><br><i>**ARC kindly provided by the author and happily received in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br></p></span>

<div id="review_604099694" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/604099694" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/604099694?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer604099694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1883375202420076388"><b>5 Bastian loving stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b7ee6978-b29a-45d5-870d-0c8e909335b5_zps6c166ac8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9725995.jpg' alt=' photo b7ee6978-b29a-45d5-870d-0c8e909335b5_zps6c166ac8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Surviving Raine</i> is a book that was released over a year ago. Yes. Over a year ago. And I have just now read it. I have no clue why it’s taken me so long. This book was just my type of read. The hero is damaged and a complete jerk most of the time. The heroine is lovable and not at all annoying. The writing is fantastic. It’s witty, steamy, full of adventure and romance. It’s quickly made it’s way on my favorites list. And it’s all because of one man. Sebastian Stark.</span>
  <span id="freeText1883375202420076388" style="display:none"><b>5 Bastian loving stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b7ee6978-b29a-45d5-870d-0c8e909335b5_zps6c166ac8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9725995.jpg" alt=" photo b7ee6978-b29a-45d5-870d-0c8e909335b5_zps6c166ac8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Surviving Raine</i> is a book that was released over a year ago. Yes. Over a year ago. And I have just now read it. I have no clue why it’s taken me so long. This book was just my type of read. The hero is damaged and a complete jerk most of the time. The heroine is lovable and not at all annoying. The writing is fantastic. It’s witty, steamy, full of adventure and romance. It’s quickly made it’s way on my favorites list. And it’s all because of one man. Sebastian Stark.<br><br>Sebastian is kind of an asshole. Alright, there is no kind of. He spends his days sailing a ship, getting drunk, smoking cigarettes and sleeping around. That is his day to day. Until one day, something changes. His ship goes under and he’s almost doesn’t make it out. But he does. Along with one of his passengers. A girl named Raine. They end up alone on a life raft after he saves her from drowning. He doesn’t know what to do with her, from the moment they first meet, she drives him crazy in the best way. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“How the fuck was I going to survive with this annoying, smoking hot bitch that I simultaneously wanted to fuck and kill?”</blockquote>
</i><br>Bastian may not know what to do with Raine, but he knows how to survive. So he’s at sea, minimal supplies, this girl is with him...he’s detoxing, she’s freaking out and wants to help, and this is his advice... (do you see why I love him so much???)<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/bd4f4593-f4b4-42f7-bf57-13cd13c6b858_zps8ab3a5e4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9725996.jpg" alt=" photo bd4f4593-f4b4-42f7-bf57-13cd13c6b858_zps8ab3a5e4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Bastain could be crude and rude, but he made me laugh out loud so many times. I was surprised with how funny parts of this book were. It wasn’t all laughs. There were lots of serious moments. The more Bastain and Raine get to know each other, the more they start to open up. Getting Bastian to open up to her is like pulling teeth. He has a sorid past and doesn’t talk about it for a reason. But when you spend day after day with the same person, you are bound to open up some. I loved that Raine really got to know Bastian. The real guy behind the asshole. Even after she learned a lot of his bad, she still cared for him and saw the good. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I’ve seen you, Bastian. I’ve seen you. Not who you pretend to be, not who you try to hide behind... I’ve seen the real you. Please, Bastian. Don’t hide him from me anymore.”</blockquote>
</i><br>It’s been a long time since Bastian has let anyone in. Especially a woman. But Raine is different. She’s special. Even though he knows he doesn’t deserve her, she is his. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/449785f9-6bb6-40f7-a1da-99b9f4fbe517_zps99603836.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9725997.jpg" alt=" photo 449785f9-6bb6-40f7-a1da-99b9f4fbe517_zps99603836.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Raine and Bastian don’t have a traditional love story. It’s a slow burn, but once they're together that slow burn turns scorching hot. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I could do it you know...I could make you come without even touching you.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Bastain and Raine have intense chemistry. But their relationship is so much more than that. Bastian makes Raine feel safe. This man who has such a violent past, makes her feel safer than she’s ever felt. For the first time in Bastian’s life. He feels wanted. Needed. He wants to be a different man for Raine, a better man. She makes him want to be better. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I don’t know how else to be. If I could be... something.... someone else... for you, I’d do it.” “I know you would.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/e0ecd51c-6518-497d-8a12-ee38140175e3_zps2c1f43a1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9725998.jpg" alt=" photo e0ecd51c-6518-497d-8a12-ee38140175e3_zps2c1f43a1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As much as I enjoyed the amusing and seductive parts of this story, what I really loved was the character growth and the emotional element. There were so many parts of this story that touched me- moved me to tears. This was one of my favorite scenes-<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <i>
    <blockquote>
      <b>“This didn't feel like I was fucking you...it was something else. I don't know what it is. I want to be with you, and touch you, and hold you. I have this overwhelming desire to protect you and make sure you're safe. Every time I look at you, it's like my chest gets crushed, and I just want to stare at you and hold on to you and tell you everything is going to be all right. I don't know what this is, Raine. I don't understand what you're doing to me."<br>I felt her fingers against my jaw and glanced down into her opened eyes. Fuck. She hadn't been asleep after all. Her mouth turned up into a beautiful smile, and her response ended me.<br><br>I love you too, Bastian.” </b>
    </blockquote>
  </i>
  <br>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/5135340a-488c-4d9f-9afb-5cefe88edb13_zpsdc80d60f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9725999.jpg" alt=" photo 5135340a-488c-4d9f-9afb-5cefe88edb13_zpsdc80d60f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>These two couldn’t be any more perfect for one another. They both give each other strength in different ways. I loved how patient and understanding Raine was with Bastian. She knew he needed someone to listen, understand and love him through all his bullshit and she did that. <br><br>And Bastian... my vulgar, sexy and broken guy. Wow. I fell hard for Sebastian Stark. So hard that he put himself right towards the top of my favorite book boyfriends list. He was just something else. He made me laugh, made me cry, made me melt and broke my heart. I couldn’t get enough of this possessive, protective, strong and damaged man. <br><br>This is a story about survival. Not just surviving the elements, but surviving life. Once I started this book I was hooked. It captivated me from the first chapter. Once I finished, I was sad it was over. There is so much more I want to say, so many things I highlighted that I left out, but there’s no way I can put it all into this review. If you get one thing out of this, don’t do the same thing I did. Don't put off reading this amazing book! If you haven’t read <i>Surviving Raine</i>- pick it up asap!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/2dbc3d08-4762-4888-a236-0ad99423e52d_zps2f4c930a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400836380i/9726000.jpg" alt=" photo 2dbc3d08-4762-4888-a236-0ad99423e52d_zps2f4c930a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/601670180" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/601670180?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=couldnt-put-down">couldnt-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=all-time-fav">all-time-fav</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer601670180" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1921368202856867712"><i>
  <b>This Book Owned Me!!!!</b>
</i><br/><i>
  <b> One Of My Favorite Books This Year!</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>If there were more stars to give- this book would have them..</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419314ra/831133.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>I read a lot of books and I've read a lot of good books.. you know how sometimes when you're reading something and all of a sudden you are like.. wow!, this is just crazy good! And your heart starts beating faster and you can't turn the pages fast enough? You feel like you are right there in the book and your emotions are just all over the place? You can't wait to re</i></span>
  <span id="freeText1921368202856867712" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>This Book Owned Me!!!!</b>
</i><br><i>
  <b> One Of My Favorite Books This Year!</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>If there were more stars to give- this book would have them..</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419314ra/831133.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I read a lot of books and I've read a lot of good books.. you know how sometimes when you're reading something and all of a sudden you are like.. wow!, this is just crazy good! And your heart starts beating faster and you can't turn the pages fast enough? You feel like you are right there in the book and your emotions are just all over the place? You can't wait to read the next page but at the same time you want to slow down and savor it because you don't want it to end? That my friends was this book for me.</i> <br><br><i>
  <b>This story is about Bastion and Raine....</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b> My Bastion....</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419314i/831134._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>Bastion owns a ship..</b>
</i><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br>He sails the carribean with a boat full of people that can afford his cruises.. He's 29 and has lived a much harder life then you or I could imagine.. He's grown up tough and has a very violent past. He's also and alcoholic and a chain smoker. He's a jerk of epic proportions and screws whores because he'd rather pay to get off then worry about having to kick someone out of his bed when its over. He's as much of an asshole as I've read in any book.. but of course our Bastion has many many layers to him....This story is told from Bastion's POV and I loved that! He's so complicated and is such an asshole.. I loved knowing all of this thoughts! He was so crazy sometimes and just to be able to be in his mind was so incredible.. Bastion is unlike any other character I've ever read. He is the ultimate anti-hero. <br><br>Raine is on his ship, The Oblation, on her own. Bastion does notice her since its his ship but doesn't really think anything of her..until an accident with the The Oblation throws them together and they must depend on each other for their lives. <br><br>I don't think I'm spoiling anything by telling you for a good while they are on a life raft together before they finally reach an uninhabited island. Bastion is an alcoholic and a chain smoker.. put that together with being a total ass and you know Raine has got her hands full with him. He's not nice and he's no gentleman. <br><br>The story revolves around them and how they learn to survive together. Thankfully Bastion knows pretty much everything about survival and for very very good reasons. He has to step up and be there for Raine because day by day he falls for her. She sees him through some enormously difficult times with his alcohol withdrawl and him just being a general dickhead most of the time. But she sees through him.. she is able to cut through all those dark brooding layers to get to the man hidden so deep within himself. They also learn that they have a very strong connection from both of their past.. and this leads you to wonder if it was coincedence that Raine just happend to be on Bastion's ship. I personally do not think this was a conincedence at all... <br><br>Although they are by themselves, there is plenty of things going on and the story never dragged at all. There was deep sadness at times as well as some very dangerous situations. I was on the edge of my seat several times freaking out wondering what was going to happen. There is also some serious steam.. they were so hot together. I re-read a few scenes several times due to how sexy they were. *fanning self*<br><br>This is my favorite book this year for sure and honestly, probably last year too. I have definitly read some good books.. but even now, after I've already finished this one, my heart still clenches just thinking about Bastion and Raine. I loved this book.. To me, this was everything a book should be. It completely swept me away. <br><br>This book does have an implied HEA and it ends with Bastion and Raine being right where they should be and I had a huge smile on my face at the end. However, the epilogue does lead me to believe there might be another book in the works that deals with someone with possible sinister intentions from Bastions past that could be very dangerous for Bastion and Raine. I really hope there will be more Raine and Bastion. My heart literally aches for more of them. <br><br>I cannot recommend this book enough!! It needs to be on your TBR list for an immediate read as soon as its released. If you love sexy jerky assholes, romance, serious steam, suspense , danger, and a love so strong in makes your heart ache.. then you do not want to pass this book up. I promise you that. <br><br><i>
  <b>One of my favorite quotes from this book...</b>
</i><br><br><i>“So long as men can breathe, or eyes can see, So long lives this, and this gives life to thee.”</i> <br><br><i>
  <b>"I give you my life, my love, my soul,” I swore to her. “As long as I’m breathing, I’m yours. Even when I’m nothing more than a fucked up dick, I still love you.”</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419215i/830849.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>The End</b>
</i><br><br><br><i> I was provied an ARC by the author in exchange for an honest review and that's what I've given here. In return, I was given the gift of one of the best books I've ever read...</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1921368202856867712" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash" class="user" itemprop="url" name="&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash" href="/user/show/5606933-that-s-all-ash">&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=badass">badass</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=i-heart">i-heart</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599241881" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8984770151225043967">There’s a moment when it comes to amazing books.<br/><br/>Whether you find it in the middle of a sentence, the last page of a chapter, or when that titanium, paper-like wire of sexual tension *finally* gives. <br/><br/>It’s the moment where you realize that the book you’re reading completely and irrevocably <i>owns</i> you.<br/><br/>So I’m going to do the one thing I hate doing: <b>I’m going to spoil this book for you, </b> by telling you that this book? <br/><br/>It has that moment.<br/><br/>You’re going to set it down. And then you’re going to find yoursel</span>
  <span id="freeText8984770151225043967" style="display:none">There’s a moment when it comes to amazing books.<br><br>Whether you find it in the middle of a sentence, the last page of a chapter, or when that titanium, paper-like wire of sexual tension *finally* gives. <br><br>It’s the moment where you realize that the book you’re reading completely and irrevocably <i>owns</i> you.<br><br>So I’m going to do the one thing I hate doing: <b>I’m going to spoil this book for you, </b> by telling you that this book? <br><br>It has that moment.<br><br>You’re going to set it down. And then you’re going to find yourself picking it right back up five minutes later (if you can last that long… personally, I only made to about 4.5). Because you just can’t be away from it for any long increments of time.<br><br>It’s the kind of book that’s going to make you have a *very intimate* relationship with your coffee maker, while simultaneously making you divorce your sparkly alarm clock.<br><br>This is your only warning.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_mi7rw6vURV1rixwdqo1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br> <br><br>♥ <b>
  <u> Bastian </u>
</b> ♥<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/marlon-teixeira-by-domenico-cennamo-02.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>The antagonistic protagonist we all love. <br><br>Let’s see… how can I best describe him…?<br><br>Oh!<br><br>Let’s say Bastian was thrown into the Hunger Games with <i>every</i> alpha/most badass/hottest character you’ve ever stumbled across.<br><br>Fifteen minutes later, Bastian would be the last one standing with a still full bottle of vodka intact to his hand, a cigarette in the other, and a slightly annoyed look on his face.<br><br>Yep. That basically sums him up..<br><br>He’s mean and crude and <i>mean</i> and crass and <b>mean</b> and<br><br>SEXY AS HELL.<br><br><i>
  <b> “I could do it, you know,” I heard myself say. My voice had dropped down low, but I knew she still heard me. I leaned over only a little, bringing my mouth closer to her ear. “I could make you come without even touching you.” </b>
</i><br><br>He’s also a captain of a small ship, which he and his best friend use to charter rich people around the world.<br><br>Until said ship sinks.<br><br>And all he’s left with is a seemingly lone young and very female survivor and a safety raft.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <u> Raine </u>
</b> ♦<br><br>The polar-opposite of Bastian.<br><br>Sweet.<br>Innocent.<br>Gentle.<br><i>Coherent</i>. <br><br>And she has utterly no idea how to handle the beast of a guy she’s suddenly stranded with.<br><br>Because without<br>•	a bottle of precious alcohol<br>•	a pack of cigs<br>•	any form of a kind word<br><br>That’s exactly what good ol’ Bastian is: a beast.<br> <br>However despite Bastian’s past career as a “fighter”, and despite his darkest secrets… Raine may be the only one who ever understood him and stood up to him.<br><br><b>
  <i> “I held you,” she said. “I held you, and you cried, and you asked me why no one had ever wanted you. You asked me why your own mother didn’t want you. You asked me why it hurt so much and if I could make it stop hurting. I may not know a lot about you, but I know you aren’t as much of a badass as you want people to think you are.” </i>
</b><br><br> <br><br>So what becomes of Bastian and Raine, the lone survivor of his sunken ship, who he can’t decide if he wants to kill or f**k?<br><br>Can he learn to trust the one person who now knows all of his secrets?<br>Can he even love her?<br>Or does he ruin the one chance at his own mental survival? <br><br><b>
  <i> “Stop shutting me out.” </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/marlon_teixeira_12__2112576026.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I never let you in baby,” I sneered. </i>
</b><br><br> <br><br>*** This ARC was kindly provided and happily received in exchange for an honest review. ***<br><br>Release Date: May 21st. ;)</span>

<div id="review_659842259" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/659842259" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/659842259?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer659842259" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8860369980190525764"><br/>This is another wildly popular contemporary. And for the most part I can understand why. The plot in simple terms: After a ship capsizes in the Caribbean the captain, Sebastian Stark and a passenger, Raine Gayle manage to escape to a life raft. Their survival at sea, and later on an island, is mainly dependent on the resourcefulness of Bastian. And of course, since this is a romance, they fall in love.<br/><br/><b>The Good</b><br/>For me, the absolute best thing about this was the survival story itself with Bastian's</span>
  <span id="freeText8860369980190525764" style="display:none"><br />This is another wildly popular contemporary. And for the most part I can understand why. The plot in simple terms: After a ship capsizes in the Caribbean the captain, Sebastian Stark and a passenger, Raine Gayle manage to escape to a life raft. Their survival at sea, and later on an island, is mainly dependent on the resourcefulness of Bastian. And of course, since this is a romance, they fall in love.<br /><br /><b>The Good</b><br />For me, the absolute best thing about this was the survival story itself with Bastian's very impressive skills being put to good use.<br /><br />The hero is not quite as bad as he seems.<br /><br />The heroine is likable and not annoying.<br /><br />The plot of the hero and heroine having to survive at sea and on an island, <i>alone</i> for the greater part of the book.<br /><br /><b>The Not-So-Good</b><br /><i>The characterisation of the hero.</i><br />I don't mind my heroes having some 'issues' or some seemingly irredeemable qualities, but this guy is a killer. For money. For sport. For gambling. Even assassins have at least some justifiable (albeit distorted) reasons for killing.<br /><br />He had a really, really bad life and there was almost nothing that didn't happen to this guy. Abandoned as a child? Yep. Numerous bad foster homes? Yep. No kindness or love? Yep. And on and on...<br /><br />He's a violent, crude, chain-smoking, angry, bad-tempered, mean-spirited, foul-mouthed, pessimistic, whinging, man-whore alcoholic.<br />But. <br />He has a master's degree in English Literature, quotes poetry and despite the abuse he heaps on his body, manages to work-out and remain fit and built. <br /><br />The repetitive angst from Bastian.<br /><br />Bastian's stamina and uber-horniness were just laughable at times.<br /><br /><i>The heroine</i><br />Raine was a little too perfect, too sweet, too innocent, too naive and too ready-with-the-perfect answer to Bastian's problems.<br /><br /><i>Other Stuff</i><br />The tournaments and killings that Bastian was involved in were just too bizarre and ridiculous to be believable.<br /><br />Not quite a cliffhanger, though the <i>to-be-continued</i> and sequel-bait is annoying and tiresome.<br /> <br /><b>My Biggest Problem</b><br />Bastian is actually <i>badass-lite.</i><br /><br />After a couple of days floating around in the raft with Bastian I definitely got the feeling he was more NA than MA. And that’s fine if you’re a reader of NA novels. <br /><br />But the guy is <b>
  <i>29 years old.</i>
</b> To me that’s a man-man. For instance, if I compared Bastian (29) to say, Gideon Cross (28), there is a lifetime of difference between these two who are essentially the same age. This is shelved as NA and it reads pretty much as NA. The heroine is twenty, so fair enough. But I really would have liked the hero to read like a twenty-nine year-old man, not a twenty year-old <i>young</i> man.<br /><br />His character simply doesn’t contain that edge of menace that I would expect from a killer. Also given his upbringing and background. He’s actually kinda sweet. <br /><br /><b>Final Thoughts</b><br />In a way comparable to the plight of TJ and Anna in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15505346.On_the_Island__On_the_Island___1_" title="On the Island (On the Island, #1) by Tracey Garvis-Graves" rel="nofollow noopener">On the Island</a>, this doesn't compare in the writing, plot or romance. But if you don't mind reading about a hero who killed-for-money, writing that is really more for the NA market with a lot of co-incidences and some implausibility, then this might suit you.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 3.5<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8860369980190525764" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_620441901" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/620441901" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/620441901?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer620441901" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18048466351174397433"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422317i/840071.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422317i/840072._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> My casting for Bastien ^^^ </i><br/><br/><u> FULL SPOILER-FREE REVIEW NOW POSTED </u><br/><br/>This was one of those random reads that just totally grabbed my attention and made me shift my TBR. I went into it not really knowing what to expect but came out of it pleasantly surprised!<br/><br/><b> It was refreshing to read such a different plot line than the usual. It was basically the story of two people stranded together on a life raft in the middle of the Caribbean struggling to survive and dealing with their growing feelings for each </b></span>
  <span id="freeText18048466351174397433" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422317i/840071.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422317i/840072._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> My casting for Bastien ^^^ </i><br><br><u> FULL SPOILER-FREE REVIEW NOW POSTED </u><br><br>This was one of those random reads that just totally grabbed my attention and made me shift my TBR. I went into it not really knowing what to expect but came out of it pleasantly surprised!<br><br><b> It was refreshing to read such a different plot line than the usual. It was basically the story of two people stranded together on a life raft in the middle of the Caribbean struggling to survive and dealing with their growing feelings for each other. </b><br><br>But… it wasn’t that simple. The hero, Bastien, (who was the captain of the ship) was a rude and crude yet lovable jerk who was also in the process of detoxing and the heroine was sweet and quiet and just his complete opposite in every way so dealing with him detoxing and them trying to survive on top of the fact that their ship just sank definitely made for an interesting story set up.<br><br>The entire story was told from Bastien’s POV. So, basically we get the perspective of the broken, drunken (now detoxing), manwhoring, badass ex-fighter. I loved it!<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “Throw her overboard or stick my tongue down her throat? I could decide and it fucking ticked me off.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>He went through a lot of change in the book. He did have some pretty low, utterly asshole moments but it was all on the outside. On the inside he was just this broken totally tortured guy who had just been completely fucked over by life and was tired of trusting people… deep down he really just wanted to be loved and I could really sense that right from the start. But… on the outside, seriously there were definitely times when I wanted to slap him. What. A. Jerk.!!<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Please stop shutting me out.”<br><br>“I never let you in, baby.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>But I’m a sucker for guys with tortured pasts… oh, and did I mentioned he was scarred? Ex-fighter… Really protective… Swoony in a really rough way. Yeah, I kinda fell for him.<br><br>I really like Raine too. Despite being sweet and shy and rather innocent, she was also quite strong and I loved that she just did NOT take his shit! I loved that she wasn’t a pushover.<br><br>But really, you couldn’t have had two more different people stuck on that raft together.<br><br>Ok, I will say this in the interest of honesty.. there were a few things that suspended my belief a little — like how quickly he opened up to her about his past given how incredibly dark it was but still, it wasn’t anything that made me disconnect from the story, more just something I noticed.<br><br>As far as the things they went through to survive, I’ve never been stranded on a boat in the middle of the ocean, but it all seemed pretty realistic to me so I liked that everything at least felt very believable from that respect.<br><br>I liked the bit of a twist to his back story. It certainly wasn’t your average ‘past’.. in fact it honestly might have been the first time I’d heard of a character being a part of something like that and I liked the way it made sense as a backstory of what had built him into the man we were seeing in the story. But seriously. It was fucked up. No wonder he drank himself into oblivion!<br><br><blockquote> <i> “I want to let you in, I just don’t know if I can.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>The book is basically very focused on two things: their survival and their growing relationship. There were a lot of survival tips and tricks. Some of them actually really interesting, and some of them seriously gross (dear freaking Lord may I never have to be in the position of needing to suck the liquid out of a fish’s eyeballs for hydration *shudders*)<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Survival 101… You can live three minutes without air, three hours without shelter, three days without water, and three weeks without food. It’s not exact, obviously, but it tells you where to put your priorities.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>But there was also a lot of focus on the relationship which eventually turned into a romance. I liked that it was slow-building and that they didn’t just fall into each other’s arms. It took its time so that by the time they got together, I believed it. I loved this part:<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I love your arms,” she said, almost too quietly for me to hear. Her fingers trailed all the way down to my wrist, then back up to my shoulder where she outlined the muscles there.<br><br>“I thought you loved my dick,” I teased.<br><br>Raine chuckled and sighed at me.<br><br>“I like that, too, but your arms are my favorite part of you. They make me feel safe.”<br><br>“I’ll always keep you safe,” I told her. I tilted my head to the side, looked into her eyes, and smiled down at her.<br><br>“I know.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>Some parts of the book felt a little “out there”, others were really sweet, and some were just downright HOT!!<br><br><blockquote> <i> “I could do it you know… I could make you come without even touching you.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>I loved the whole angle of the broken hero, utterly fucked over by life, a true survivor, and yet with zero self worth being shown how to trust love by this girl who saw right through his facade into the real him and brought out the best in him and made him feel safe, loved and worthy.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “As long as I’m breathing, I’m yours. Even when I’m nothing more than a fucked up dick, I still love you.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>What is it about the grouchy crude, rude, lovable badass jerks that just melt our hearts?? There were times when I couldn’t help but smile.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “What did you do before sailing?”<br><br>Here was a topic best avoided.<br><br>“Not much.”<br><br>“You must have done something.”<br><br>“Not necessarily.”<br><br>“Well you had to have done something to be able to buy your boat, right?”<br><br>“It’s a ship. Or it was. Boats are small, and size fucking matters.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br>LOL. I loved that Raine was strong, but just in a very quiet way. Yes, she had moments of naivete but not stupidity and I respected that difference.<br><br>Emotionally, this was really a journey of feeling worthy of and finding love. Physically, it was a journey of survival.<br><br>There is no relationship cliffhanger however there are still really big bad guys out there who will likely try and come after them so I’m looking forward to the next one but have no doubt that they’ll remain strong together as a couple.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I love you… I’ll never walk away from you, Raine, I swear — I’ll be with you as long as you will have me.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>I really enjoyed my read and if you just want something really different, this would definitely be one to consider. There were a few slow parts but at the same time, looking back on it, there weren’t any parts I’d want to take out either and during my read, I couldn’t put it down. <br><br>It was just a total chance of pace from my normal reads and sometimes that’s exactly what you need :-)<br><br>4+ stars (maybe 4.5 in certain places)<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a> </b><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1367074353l/17447588.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> As the captain of a schooner catering to the elite on the Caribbean Seas, Sebastian Stark does his best to avoid any human encounters. Interacting with people isn’t his thing, and he prefers the company of a bottle of vodka, a shot glass, and maybe a whore. There’s no doubt he’s hiding from a checkered past, but he does well keeping everything to himself…<br><br>…until the night his schooner capsizes, and he’s stuck on a life raft with one of the passengers.<br><br>Raine’s young, she’s cute, and Bastian would probably be into her if he wasn’t suffering from alcohol withdrawal. As the days pass, DTs, starvation, and dehydration become the norm. Even the most closed person starts to open up when he thinks he’s going to die, but when she realizes their traumatic pasts are connected, it’s no longer the elements that have Bastian concerned.<br><br>He has no idea how he’s going to Survive Raine.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="18048466351174397433" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer612152895" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11626133977623288799">4.5 STARS<br/><br/>This is the story about Raine and Sebastian (Bastian) … Bastian is the captain of a boat, <i>The Oblation</i>. The boat hits some sort of storm and it sinks but not before Bastian gets the emergency raft afloat. He sees a body in the water and hauls it on board. It is Raine, sweet Raine and their journey takes them onto the open seas to a deserted island where they have to survive the elements. Bastin is an alcoholic so we see him going through withdrawl symptoms, DTs, etc. It is fairly heartb</span>
  <span id="freeText11626133977623288799" style="display:none">4.5 STARS<br><br>This is the story about Raine and Sebastian (Bastian) … Bastian is the captain of a boat, <i>The Oblation</i>. The boat hits some sort of storm and it sinks but not before Bastian gets the emergency raft afloat. He sees a body in the water and hauls it on board. It is Raine, sweet Raine and their journey takes them onto the open seas to a deserted island where they have to survive the elements. Bastin is an alcoholic so we see him going through withdrawl symptoms, DTs, etc. It is fairly heartbreaking. Raine is there with him every step of the way. He has been a loner much of his life. They open up to each other – there is an underlying side story also regarding her father. She is, I think 20 years old, to his 30. I loved this story. I loved the love scenes, I loved the survival tactics they had to use. Loved how Sebastian opened up to Raine…. A wonderful read and I suppose it was sort of an abrupt ending but it definitely paved the way for another story from these two wonderful people. I see that there is another book due out in 2014 so look forward to reading further about Bastian and Raine…. Get the feeling it will not be an easy road they will have to travel.<br><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836193.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380810539ra/3124416.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><b>For once it wasn’t just me I needed to look after. I was pretty confident I could survive in a life raft for quite some time, but survive Raine without my cock jumping straight out of my shorts like a divining rod? Not so sure.</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836195._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"I don’t do relationships," I told her. "I try to keep things a little easier. No flowers, no commitments. Just fucking "</b><br><br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836196.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"Tell me you got me!"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836197._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"I’d die without you Bastian. Even if I lived, I’d die inside."</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836198.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <b>"Forgiveness is the fragrance of the violet which still clings fast to the heel that crushed it."</b><br><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836199.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>With her I could have a real life, without the constant threat of pain. I’d lived through a lot of shit. I’d survived abandonment, betrayal, endless violence, and the elements, but could I survive Raine? Could I live with her, in her world like a regular person? Was I strong enough to do that?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421108i/836200._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380810539i/3124417.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/622622122?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer622622122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10747257615071470648"><b>
  <blockquote>"Forgiveness is the fragrance of the violet which still clings fast to the heel that crushed it. "Raine's eyes met mine again, her tears still staining her cheeks. "I'm a heel, Raine," I told her. "You're my beautiful violet and I'm always crushing you..."</blockquote>
</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422636i/841232.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>Hey...little disclaimer here...I know there is talk of this book having a cliffie (most of you know how I feel about cliffhangers), but I really don't think this ends in a cliffie AT ALL! The story told within this book is <i>complete</i>....I p</span>
  <span id="freeText10747257615071470648" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>"Forgiveness is the fragrance of the violet which still clings fast to the heel that crushed it. "Raine's eyes met mine again, her tears still staining her cheeks. "I'm a heel, Raine," I told her. "You're my beautiful violet and I'm always crushing you..."</blockquote>
</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422636i/841232.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Hey...little disclaimer here...I know there is talk of this book having a cliffie (most of you know how I feel about cliffhangers), but I really don't think this ends in a cliffie AT ALL! The story told within this book is <i>complete</i>....I put it down with a nice sigh and a finished feeling. That being said, the epilogue is a bit of a teaser for the next book...almost as if the author added a teaser chapter from the next in the series.<br><br>Surviving Raine: I survived it! It was more of a Surviving Sebastian Stark for me, though...my lips are bitten to shreds and I think my heart stopped a couple of times, but I'm still here.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"I'm a nutcase, Raine," I told her. "I'm a murderer and a drunk. I use women as a place to stick my cock. That's who I am. You don't want to delude yourself into thinking I'm something else."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>MY SYNOPSIS:</u>
</b><br>This is told entirely from the male point of view....which I LOVED!!!!! I don't think being inside of Raine's head would have lent me to being able to understand Sebastian the way I needed to in order to empathize with him. <br><br>Sabastian Stark is living a hard life of drinking and f*cking, sleeping, and captaining his ship that totes around rich party people from tropical paradise to tropical paradise. But he enjoys none of it, living his own personal hell of a daily grind and nights filled with nightmares. Only these nightmares were once reality for him. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422636i/841233.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When he is awakened one night from his drunken slumber by literally crashing into the ceiling of his cabin, his first thought is to get the life rafts afloat for his passengers. Finding the rafts gone and the passengers gone as well, he hopes for the best and takes for himself the tiny emergency raft that he and his shipmate had added on a whim a few months ago. <br><br>But as he watches his ship sink into the ocean, he spots a figure sinking into the waves right along with it. <br><br>Here is our first glimpse of the true nature of the conundrum that is Sebastian Stark... He jumps out of the safety of his raft and saves a life, allowing Raine to survive. Now, if only Sebastian can survive Raine...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422636i/841234._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS:</u>
</b><br>Wow...pretty much sums it up...I tend to like the antihero to begin with, and if you like sweet guys who are tender with their woman, I don't suggest reading this...or at least I suggest reading this with an open mind and FINISH it before judging Sebastian too harshly. He's pretty much fifty shades of messed up...his past is just about as horrible as it gets for a kid, but you don't get to know him for quite awhile, so you only get the nasty, mean, and selfish Sebastian. As the story wears on...and the alcohol wears off...he slowly opens up to Raine.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"I didn't know how to stop. Everything in my body was so tight - so tense and hard - I couldn't even stop if I wanted to - I was on complete, reactionary autopilot. I managed to wrap my arms around my knees and lean forward a little, bt that was it. I couldn't look at her because if I did my reaction would be - undoubtedly - violent. <i>I would either lash out more with verbal abuse or I would grab her and violently...beg her to hold me. Fuck..."</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br>Raine...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422636i/841235.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>She's such a sweetheart! At first, almost too sweet for Bastien, but we come to learn that she has one hell of a backbone...this girl takes Sebastian's crap over and over again, and yet she still sees the good in him, forgives him almost instantly, because she can see his inner turmoil, and she knows he's a good person. I loved Raine! I loved how she starts off very scared and timid, and slowly gains confidence and spunk as the story wears on and her circumstances force her into dealing with more than she ever thought she could. And yet she still breaks down...a couple of times, and I love that too...women can be vulnerable and yet still be strong. And Raine exemplifies that, especially as her love for Bastien continues to be stronger and stronger. It's that steadfast nature of hers that slowly brings out his humanity. It's at once painful and beautiful to read.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I'd fucked thirty year veteran whores and barely out of high school virgins. Some felt better than others, but it wasn't the physical that made it different. When I connected with Raine physically, I could feel every bit of her soul within my own...<i>It had never occurred to me before that I might have a soul..."</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br>One big redeeming quality for Sebastian is that he never, ever puts his life before Raine's...it's paramount to him that she survive, even in the beginning, before he loves her. He's a good person, somewhere in the dark recesses of what his life SHOULD have been, he's a good person. And he KNOWS that he's messed up...what he learns from Raine, and what he has to learn to accept, is that there is good in him as well...that he's worthy of love and affection just as much as she is. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422636i/841236._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I knew she wanted me. I knew she loved me. The single, brightest point in the universe wanted and loved me."</blockquote>
</b> </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3420789093" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8559003662151492144"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Who would say no to an inestimable period of self isolation if it meant getting stranded on an island with <b>Sebastian Stark</b> who was the very definition of a damaged good with pockets of sweetness and who would give you special treatments, such as:<br/><br/><blockquote>- giving you free lessons on how to survive on a lifeboat and keeping you alive with his resourcefulness<br/>- protecting you from any kind of danger with his deadly fighting skills<br/>- helping you maintain your feminine hygiene (including but not limit</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8559003662151492144" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br /><br />Who would say no to an inestimable period of self isolation if it meant getting stranded on an island with <b>Sebastian Stark</b> who was the very definition of a damaged good with pockets of sweetness and who would give you special treatments, such as:<br /><br /><blockquote>- giving you free lessons on how to survive on a lifeboat and keeping you alive with his resourcefulness<br />- protecting you from any kind of danger with his deadly fighting skills<br />- helping you maintain your feminine hygiene (including but not limited to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[shaving your armpits and legs, sacrificing his boxer briefs for you, building you a self made fresh water generator type of thing <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>)<br />- fulfilling your (and his) other needs by indulging you in titillating sweat inducing activities???</blockquote><br />That was a long ass question, but the answer is, NOT ME!!! Despite his <i>extremely</i> difficult, unlikeable, downright despicable personality and questionable morale, Bastian grew on me little by little and became an easy character to love.<br /><br /><blockquote>✓ Soft and hard<br />✓ Troubled and tortured<br />✓ Foul mouthed but fluent at Shakespeare<br />✓ Caveman possessive but endearing instead of overbearing<br />✓ Bad tempered but sweet and gentle when in love</blockquote><br />God, I’m obsessed with him!<br /><br />The book was told from the male’s POV. The story was absolutely engrossing, heartfelt and funny at times, whilst also bursting with chemistry, tension, and sexiness at others. Raine was the perfect match for Bastian with her being everything he was not. I was almost sad when they were rescued and had to leave the island.<br /><br />More than half a decade since <i>Surviving Raine</i> was published, and I’d just now discovered what a ride this was. Thank you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/74099824-bee" rel="nofollow noopener">Bee</a> for sharing Bastian with me. My review sucks and is insufficient to how I actually felt, but I treasured every second of this book.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=hero-drunk">hero-drunk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=heroine-passive">heroine-passive</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=survival-story">survival-story</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769300006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8052266593746894898"><br/><b>Not my cuppa. Honestly, I am really getting sick of this formula!</b><br/><br/>Bastian was yet another asshole hero, much like Travis from Beautiful Disaster, who drinks too much, smokes too much, curses too much, fights too much, feels he doesn't deserve to be loved, and alternates treating his heroine like a piece of shit or a priceless golden statuesque goddess. <br/><br/>Raine was yet another doormat, doe-eyed, virginal innocent, giggly heroine with a speech impediment, (this one couldn't talk without inserting an </span>
  <span id="freeText8052266593746894898" style="display:none"><br /><b>Not my cuppa. Honestly, I am really getting sick of this formula!</b><br /><br />Bastian was yet another asshole hero, much like Travis from Beautiful Disaster, who drinks too much, smokes too much, curses too much, fights too much, feels he doesn't deserve to be loved, and alternates treating his heroine like a piece of shit or a priceless golden statuesque goddess. <br /><br />Raine was yet another doormat, doe-eyed, virginal innocent, giggly heroine with a speech impediment, (this one couldn't talk without inserting an "...uhm..." every few sentences), who believes in rainbows and unicorns, that love will conquer all, and that heroes like Bastian are just 'being silly' when they repeatedly treat them with abusive language and actions. <br /><br />The relationship is essentially them fighting, fucking, fighting, fucking, fighting, then more fucking and more fighting. Toss in a few "I love you's" and a boatload of the heroine telling the hero he is worthy of love, and you have just summed it all up. <br /><br />And to round out the formula, this story is going to be dragged into yet more books. <br /><br />The shipwreck and survival aspects were my favorite part of this story, and it is why I bothered to finish the book. Despite not liking or believing in these two, I enjoyed seeing how they worked to survive, and I did want to know if or how they were rescued.<br /><br />I know this book is really popular, and I understand that. I think this book is well suited for readers who like their romance characters similar to ones found in Beautiful Disaster and Fifty Shades, which I do not. Otherwise, I wouldn't recommend this one. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8052266593746894898" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText9352105882016799371" style="display:none"><b>4,5 you're-my-home ⭐️'s</b><br><br><b>Song:</b> <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eLaNBbKJPfw" rel="nofollow noopener">Mr. Probz - Nothing Really Matters </a>. This song is <b>so</b> them it's scary!!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You got me?” <br>“Yeah, I got you.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><i>From now on :<br>Anyone : If you were stranded on an island what would you bring ? <br>Me : Easy. <b>Sebastian Stark. </b><br>Anyone : <b>WHAT</b> not <b>WHO</b>!<br>Me : like I said, Sebastian Stark. 🙃<br>Anyone : You obviously don't understand the question 🤬<br>Me : You obviously don't know Sebastian Stark. 😅</i><br><br>Starting this book, I was promised the asshole of all assholes.<br> <b>Sebastian Stark</b> definitely more than delivered on that end. He was a <b>straight up dick, with a despicable personality and a huge chip on his shoulder. </b><br>But what you, cruel cruel people, obviously <b>forgot to tell me was how broken and tortured he was, how much my heart would break for him and how sweet and gentle he could be. </b>🥺<br><br>I'm not gonna go into details about what happens because :<br><br>1. This book released 7 years ago, I'm basically one of the last people to read it. That rock I was living under was really heavy, btw. <br>2. There are many incredible reviews that go into detail about everything. <br>3. All you really need to know is in the blurb, anyway.<br><br>When I got to this part <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“There was something wrong with me, and none of them ever wanted me to stay.  They’d keep the other kids.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I was really<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594143411ra/29776571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And to him<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594143411ra/29776572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and to whoever dared to make him feel unwanted and unlovable <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594143411ra/29776570.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before he fell for Raine, Sebastian was a sarcastic, funny but really mean jerk. Once he fell in love, he was still kind of a jerk, but the sweetest, gentlest, most clueless but lovable jerk. 🥺<br>What pre-love and post-love Sebastian had in common tho, was the <b>deep underlying vulnerability</b> that jumped off the pages at me and held me by the throat for a good chunk of the book. <br>My heart shattered for him and he kept pulling at the remaining strings, as if me just laying there brokenhearted and plotting the demise of an entire fictional organisation wasn't enough for him.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“ This didn’t feel like I was fucking you…it was something else.  I don’t know what it is.  I want to be with you, and touch you, and hold you.  I have this overwhelming desire to protect you and make sure you’re safe.  Every time I look at you, it’s like my chest gets crushed, and I just want to stare at you and hold on to you and tell you everything is going to be all right.  I don’t know what this is, Raine.  I don’t understand what you’re doing to me.”<br>“I love you too, Bastian.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>While the highlight of this book for me was definitely him, <b>Raine</b> still stood her own against him. She was resilient, soft with a backbone of steel, but not the in-your-face kind. <br>She really was perfect for him, <b>the calm to his storm</b>. <br>And he was perfect for her, <b>her anchor in the rain (like really heavy rain, deluge/storm but I'm lame and I'm trynna word play so rain it is)</b>.<br><br>Now, I've read the spoilers for the second book <i>(don't look at me like that, we've already established I'm a cheat)</i> and someone needs to tell Shay Savage that the fact that they don't have kids is <b>NOT OKAY. AT ALL. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594143410ra/29776569.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
