<div id="review_623687410" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/623687410" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/623687410?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer623687410" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14095374759237386758"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391427807i/8386676.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Let me tell you my thoughts and feelings about this magnificent story....</i><br/><br/>Sebastian Stark likes to lose himself in his vices.... A whore and a bottle, or ten, of something alcoholic. That's his life: women, alcohol, nicotine and living on the sea, in his beloved ship, The Oblation.<i> He wants nothing more from his existence.....</i><br/><br/><b>"I was what I was - violent, crude, and utterly unlovable."</b> <i> Well lets just see about that shall we?</i><br/><br/>One day it all goes wrong, the ship capsizes and Sebastian finds himself</span>
  <span id="freeText14095374759237386758" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391427807i/8386676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Let me tell you my thoughts and feelings about this magnificent story....</i><br><br>Sebastian Stark likes to lose himself in his vices.... A whore and a bottle, or ten, of something alcoholic. That's his life: women, alcohol, nicotine and living on the sea, in his beloved ship, The Oblation.<i> He wants nothing more from his existence.....</i><br><br><b>"I was what I was - violent, crude, and utterly unlovable."</b> <i> Well lets just see about that shall we?</i><br><br>One day it all goes wrong, the ship capsizes and Sebastian finds himself alone, on a raft, with Raine, a female passenger.<br><br>How will she deal with Bastian??? How will he cope without his vices???<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391523484i/8404969._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They’re in an unusual situation and everything is heightened. Time emotions, tempers, feelings. Everything is intensified and it makes for an extremely powerful story. They have so much time to learn about each other.... To make discoveries.... So much more time to think, so many inner thoughts. Because of the scenario, their confinement.... <i>Everything slows down.</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400613607i/9697241._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sebastian is quite an amusing guy. I love his sarcastic mouth; his personality shines through the writing in immeasurable ways. He's macho, stubborn, determined. He would fight to the death until he won. He has an “incredible will to survive.” He's not all hearts and flowers, and romance.... <i>Far from it.</i> He's done some terrible things in his life, seen and experienced violence, betrayal and abandonment....His life story is intense. It's dark, it's gruesome, it's mind blowing, and insanely dangerous. There are things he needs to lose from his mind, there a dreams he needs to ward off. Bastian had a hideous start to life and, frankly, it never really got any better. He has a very quick temper, he's beyond irritable without his vices and it causes a lot of problems. <br><br>There are <i>Dreams…..</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I held you, and you cried, and you asked me why no one had ever wanted you." </b>
</blockquote><br>Raine is a beautiful girl, she's strong and resilient and courageous. Everything she says is honest and pure, so when she speaks, you know she means it with every fiber of her being. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b> “I’d die without you, Bastian. Even if I lived, I’d die inside.”</b>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <i>That line just got to my heart and squeezed.</i> She's amazing at drawing him out, tending to him.... Bringing out the best.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391521757i/8404649._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Sebastian's voice</u><br>Surviving Rain is all told from Sebastian's point of view and, for almost the entire time, it's just Sebastian and Raine on the page. It's magical genius….. <i>Simply sublime.</i> In her voice he may have seemed harsh and cruel…. But we hear how he feels about <i>everything.</i> We see glimpses of his past… The reasons why??? <br><br><b>So many beautiful moments...</b><i><br> His words sometimes took my breath away…..</i><br><br><i>So many….OMG..<i>Why</i> moments???</i><br><br>His inner thoughts are just that, his mind pouring out, limitlessly, his thoughts, his dreams, his feelings. There's no filter and this is the beauty of the story. He's a brute on the outside, he sometimes does and says things that aren't nice but we, the reader, see into his soul and his soul is wonderful.... He has so many facets to him. So many qualities, some are hidden but Raine draws them out. He's strong, powerful, raw, harsh but the author gives us light and shade. Makes him individual. Gives his tough guy image an alter ego. It's stunning characterization. <br><br><i>It gave me goosebumps...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391513937i/8403247._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Paradise.....</i><br>When they are together physically it’s not only smoking hot **I was fanning myself** but powerful in the extreme. It was deep, sexy, erotic and intense… Their connection and intensity towards each other is palpable.<i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391514599i/8403386._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How will their situation be resolved??? </i><br><br><b>
  <i>Surviving Raine </i>
</b>took me through a range of emotions. Happy, sad, fearful, intrigue. It made me smile and cry. It's intense and gripping. There’s heartfelt discussions... But it never once felt overly sentimental. The tone is perfect, the characters so authentically developed, the dialogue stunningly naturalistic. The effortless writing is classy and powerfully moving; it filled me with so many feelings.<br><br>Sebastian is a survivor in life but....<br><br><b>
  <i>How will he Survive Raine</i>
</b> <br><br>Read this epic book and find out for yourself. You will love!!!<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Perhaps the real question here is how could he survive without her? <b> “As long as I’m breathing, I’m yours.” “I’ll always keep you safe.”~ Bastian</b>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b></b><i> My heart melts when he speaks..... </i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384904420ra/7024025.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I can't wait for more</i><br><br>♥BR with Andrea, thanks for a great buddy read, lady xxx<br><i> I can't wait for the next book. I wonder if any of our thoughts and wishes will come true??? </i><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_599385534" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/599385534" />
    <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha"><img alt="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528597635p2/15735368.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599385534" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10731852440200640637"><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/20/savagesurvivingrainetit.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418975i/830063.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★! Surviving Raine, book 1. Two lonely & broken people waiting to be rescued from ship-wreck face danger & dismal conditions, yet their biggest obstacles are their demons within.</b><br/><br/><b>Surviving Raine is the story of Bastian and Raine who end up shipwrecked</b> on a 10 foot emergency raft after Bastian’s schooner, Oblation capsizes in the Caribbean Sea. Dire weather conditions and limited supplies of food, water, alcohol and cigarettes put them on a collision course with disaster as an injured Basti</span>
  <span id="freeText10731852440200640637" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/20/savagesurvivingrainetit.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418975i/830063.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★! Surviving Raine, book 1. Two lonely &amp; broken people waiting to be rescued from ship-wreck face danger &amp; dismal conditions, yet their biggest obstacles are their demons within.</b><br><br><b>Surviving Raine is the story of Bastian and Raine who end up shipwrecked</b> on a 10 foot emergency raft after Bastian’s schooner, Oblation capsizes in the Caribbean Sea. Dire weather conditions and limited supplies of food, water, alcohol and cigarettes put them on a collision course with disaster as an injured Bastian is forced to detox leaving Raine to take care of him and keeping them alive. Both Bastian and Raine have trouble pasts. Once Bastian wakes up a friendship is forged and a romance ensues while their past comes back to haunt them. They are faced with danger and many set-backs while they are waiting to be rescued. But they are also rewarded as secrets are uncovered. <b>Their story is a journey of self-discovery, making peace with one’s demons and taking a chance on love</b>.<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/17/savagesurvivingraine1he.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418975i/830064.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Bastian Stark</b> aka Daniel is the Captain and owner of Oblation. For the last couple of years his life has been spinning out of control with him constantly drunk. He’s lucky to have the help and support of his two friends to run his cruise business. He has reasons for his self-destructive behavior and we learn more about his heart-wrenching childhood and his demons as the story unfolds Bastian the child had nothing handed to him and the lost child is still apparent in Bastian the man.<br><br>Five words to describe Bastian: <b>Sarcastic, broken, sexy, brooding and protective</b>.<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/692/savagesurvivingraine1he.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418975i/830065.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Raine Gayle</b> also has demons to deal with, albeit more recent. She was a lost soul just drifting through life and taking this cruise was supposed to be the start of a new beginning. As odd as it may sound, ending up ship-wrecked with Bastian might have been the best thing that could have happened to her.<br><br>Five words to describe Raine: <b>Sweet, unassuming, loyal, lonely and private</b>.<br><br><i>My only grievance was that the middle of the story was at times a little too detailed and longwinded.</i><br><br>Surviving Raine is told from Bastian’s POV and the book title indicates his frustration and fear surviving the shipwreck and his struggle with Raine, who he feels an instant attraction to. As they are waiting to be rescued, Bastian is focused on survival while Raine becomes more and more determined to save Bastian from the demons of his past. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Don’t touch me,” I clarified. <br>“Why not?” <br>Because I want it and I don’t deserve it….”<br><br>***<br>“Your…acceptance of me,” I said. “That’s really my favorite thing about you. I don’t know why you put up with my shit, but I’m glad you do.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>For me it was a treat to get a story written from the hero’s POV. Both Bastian and Raine are wonderful and you’ll find yourself rooting for them to make I through and to get their HEA.</b><br><br>I am happy to report that this is not the end of their story. Book 1 leaves them in a good place, but in the epilogue, unbeknownst to them both, there is danger lurking. <u>Book 2 is expected to be released sometime in 2014.</u><br><br>***<br>Hero rating: 4.5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 4 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 4 stars<br>Story ending rating: 3 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this book: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><br>Be sure to check out this <b>ReCap,</b> DICKtation of the May 30th <b>
  <a href="https://goo.gl/LVQSAM" rel="nofollow noopener">SPOTlight on Shay Savage LIVE chat</a>
</b> on Shh… [Smut, Heroes &amp; HEAs…] with Alessandra!<br><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided to me by author in exchange for an honest review.</i>

<div id="review_604029117" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/604029117" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/604029117?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer604029117" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8885733954621442234">Re-reading 5-20-14 in prep for sequel. <br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/d3dd5c84b7b7bc2f19dbd68c6bd3a4d7_zps3563b863.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419681i/832355._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo d3dd5c84b7b7bc2f19dbd68c6bd3a4d7_zps3563b863.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Dear Bastian,<br/>Wow. Words cannot express the feelings your story evoked in me. It was your story to tell and I thank you for sharing. Your childhood was obviously horrible. I cannot fathom how your parents left a poor child alone in this world. Why the foster care parents abandoned you one by one was even further disheartening. I can see why this caused you such feelings of worthlessness and made you the fighter you had to be in life. You did horrible thi</span>
  <span id="freeText8885733954621442234" style="display:none">Re-reading 5-20-14 in prep for sequel. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/d3dd5c84b7b7bc2f19dbd68c6bd3a4d7_zps3563b863.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419681i/832355._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo d3dd5c84b7b7bc2f19dbd68c6bd3a4d7_zps3563b863.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Dear Bastian,<br>Wow. Words cannot express the feelings your story evoked in me. It was your story to tell and I thank you for sharing. Your childhood was obviously horrible. I cannot fathom how your parents left a poor child alone in this world. Why the foster care parents abandoned you one by one was even further disheartening. I can see why this caused you such feelings of worthlessness and made you the fighter you had to be in life. You did horrible things, Bastian, but, believe it or not, I understand you. It was survival of the fittest from day one but that mentality made you the man you needed to be to survive the shipwreck of your schooner. How you knew how to survive in that little lifeboat with very little,food and water is beyond me! You not only saved yourself, but saved Raine time and again those sixty-some days after the boat capsized. Your only instinct was to save Raine...and you didn't even know who she was at the time. You would've given your life for her survival, wouldn't you Bastian? That makes you a GOOD guy. Yes, you're crass, foul-mouthed with emotional walls built up so high. I get it. You thought Raine couldn't climb those walls.....but there's something you should know- NEVER underestimate a woman, Bastian. I do think you can Survive Raine. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Male%20Eye%20Candy/605d0ac7039518ee10bceee64d74cc92_zpsa2ca7957.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419681i/832356._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 605d0ac7039518ee10bceee64d74cc92_zpsa2ca7957.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Dearest Raine,<br> You are awesome! You were strong, took the shit that was delivered when your father was killed and moved the heck on. When life threw you another blow on that luxury schooner trip, you survived. Your tenacity in times where anyone else would give up is remarkable. The fact you didn't throw that beastly Bastian over that life raft was remarkable in itself. Good self control, my dear. But you saw beyond that hard, scarred exterior....you saw the child that was left alone in this world. You saw his need to protect himself from that fear of abandonment...of worthlessness. You let him lash out, got him through his alcohol withdrawal, worked as a team until finally, finally you were found. You loved Bastian for the person he was deep down and I truly feel you saved his life. He used to live for his next drink but now he lives for you. His quote<i> "If you call forth what is in you, it will save you. If you do not call forth what is in you, it will destroy you." </i>The was for you. You gave him the strength to power on. This was Bastian's story...a story of bad times, poor choices, horrible mistakes....and second chances to make for good times and good choices. He will still make mistakes, say hurtful things, and you know it but amazingly, you understand him. Your strength is commendable Raine. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Women%20for%20reviews/567491523ad1dbcb07018fa34dee8c74_zps7da67039.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419681i/832357._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 567491523ad1dbcb07018fa34dee8c74_zps7da67039.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Dearest Shay Savage-<br> Thank you, thank you, thank you for sharing this story with me. I loved it. It was seriously like a movie in my head- an action packed thriller/romance in one! Your character development of both Bastian and Raine was stellar! Bastian did HORRIBLE things in his past, acted like a complete ass the first quarter of the book and you still managed to make me fall in love with that tortured soul. <br> Thank you for giving me a STRONG heroine in Raine. With the loss of her father, her ship capsizing and being stranded with a raving lunatic/alcoholic, she cried, but she got tough. This book was about survival not only physically but I'm coming away with a feeling of good things for these two. I see major danger in their midst with your epilogue but I have faith they'll make it through anything. Again, the book was awesome. It had everything I crave in a good solid plot- and the anti-hero aspect is my favorite. Thank you for the opportunity to read an arc, Shay.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/da27a2315a18e19fca417d08e4734bc9_zps5009bc8e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419681i/832358._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo da27a2315a18e19fca417d08e4734bc9_zps5009bc8e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Bravo!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/Applause%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419681ra/832359.gif" alt="Applause gifs photo: applause applause.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>***Story ends in a HFN (happy for now) but the epilogue had some issues lurking in the shadows. Not a cliffy!<br><br><i>Arc provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer603207140" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13535978498523269533"><b>4.5 I guess I really do love the assholes after all Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404766714i/10279899._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I'm not...a nice guy, Raine." I didn't know how to make her understand that there wasn't anything else to me despite what she wanted to believe. I was what I was- violent, crude, and utterly unlovable."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396151411i/9095735.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>First, if you haven't yet read any books by this author, you need to get out from under the rock you've been living under and GET ON IT. Really. Shay Savage is the queen of male POV and this book just further proves it.<br/><br/><b>Meet Sebas</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13535978498523269533" style="display:none"><b>4.5 I guess I really do love the assholes after all Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404766714i/10279899._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I'm not...a nice guy, Raine." I didn't know how to make her understand that there wasn't anything else to me despite what she wanted to believe. I was what I was- violent, crude, and utterly unlovable."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396151411i/9095735.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>First, if you haven't yet read any books by this author, you need to get out from under the rock you've been living under and GET ON IT. Really. Shay Savage is the queen of male POV and this book just further proves it.<br><br><b>Meet Sebastian Stark:</b><br>Alcoholic<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405024331ra/10327908.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Chain smoker<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405024331ra/10327909.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Killer<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405024331ra/10327910.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And a grade A asshole<br><br>Intrigued, aren't you?<br><br>Bastian is trying to put his past behind him, but the only way to drown out the voices of demons past is with alcohol and countless faceless women...even if he has to pay for them<br><br>He doesn't want to know anyone, and he certainly doesn't want anyone to know him. So he spends his days a the captain of a schooner that caters to the rich and elite, and his nights drinking himself into a oblivion<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405024331ra/10327911.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But then he wakes up to a storm, a sinking ship, and finds himself stuck on a lifeboat with one of the passengers who also happens to temp him in two different directions<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Toss her overboard or stick my tongue down her throat? I couldn't decide and it fucking ticked me off.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405024331i/10327912._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now me being the huge fan of the assholes that I am, I fell head over heels for Bastian from the very firs page. But if you're the sort that needs convincing, allow me to present exhibit A:<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I told you before. I'm fucking tense"<br>"Well, is there something I can do to help with that? Or are you just going to yell at me all this time?<br>"Yeah, there is something you can do," I said coldly, turning my glare at her. "Come here and blow me. That would probably ease a bit of my tension- especially if you swallow."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>or exhibit B<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">...my cock was in danger of busting right through the buttons of my shorts and maybe taking a little trip all on his own. I had the feeling he was already contacting "AAA" for a Triptik and probably trying to book a hotel in pussyland.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Stuck with a woman that equal parts soothes his damaged soul and reminds him of everything he can never be is a constant state for Bastian. Your heart will absolutely break for him. He may be a growly, vulgar asshole, but beneath all that is the heart of man that is just begging for love.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I didn't want her to touch me even if my brain was screaming for it. She shouldn't want to have her hands on me. I was fucking toxic- ask any woman who knew me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Little by little Bastian begins to open up to Raine and divest more and more of his past. And holy shit, his past!<br>Raine, in her understated way slowly chips away at all his defenses and walls. And let me tell you, when this man finally allows himself to fall? <b>Damn.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I felt everything as I let her take me- mind, body and soul. I did't know if she wanted it or needed it like I did, but I gave it to her anyway.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401230188ra/9773375.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But don't worry, even when he falls and his possessive and sweet side comes out, he never quite loses that edge of vulgar asshole that I've come to love about him<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Vulgar?" I mocked surprise, placing my hand over my chest. "You're implying my speech might include vulgarities? You fucking take that shit back right now!"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Surviving Raine is told solely in Bastian's POV and it's a book that you'll be unable to set down. Or at least I wasn't. Shay Savage has this way to her writing that never fails to suck you into the story and keep you riveted until the last page. She also writes some of the best anti-heroes I've had the pleasure of reading about.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405024331i/10327913._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I can tell you I'm very glad I waited until book two was out to read this. The cliffhanger isn't terrible, but it is there, and it's obvious there's a whole lot more to be found out. And I. Cannot. Freaking. WAIT!<br><br><i>P.S.<br>Thank you to the lovely Joanna for finally giving me the push I needed and challenging me to read this little gem &lt;3</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13535978498523269533" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3421476956?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" href="/user/show/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus">Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=adult-romance">adult-romance</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3421476956" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3660711945931218631"><b>3.5 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Don't cry, Raine. Not for me."<br/>"Someone should."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Sebastian Stark!! His possessive and obsessive ways stole my heart. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"As long as I'm breathing, I'm yours. Even when I'm nothing more than a fucked up dick, I still love you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <b>Plot in a nutshell:</b> this quote sums it up perfectly . . .<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We were in a life raft, for the love of God, in the middle of the fucking Caribbean, and I was getting a hard on from a half-drowned stranger lying on top of me. Well at least </b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3660711945931218631" style="display:none"><b>3.5 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Don't cry, Raine. Not for me."<br />"Someone should."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Sebastian Stark!! His possessive and obsessive ways stole my heart. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"As long as I'm breathing, I'm yours. Even when I'm nothing more than a fucked up dick, I still love you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <b>Plot in a nutshell:</b> this quote sums it up perfectly . . .<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We were in a life raft, for the love of God, in the middle of the fucking Caribbean, and I was getting a hard on from a half-drowned stranger lying on top of me. Well at least we know I'm still a guy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>I love a good survival story! Honestly, I don't know how I hadn't stumbled onto this book before now.<br /><br />And I did enjoy it . . . <br /><br />However, I wished that Raine had been given a bigger part. Since the book focused on Sebastian and his backstory, I felt like I didn't get to know her. It was as if her only purpose was to showcase the Hero. <br /><br />And I kept getting distracted by the details that didn't sit well with me . . . here are just a few examples . . . <b>minor spoilers ahead:</b><br /><br />Things like salt water, no showers, no toothbrushes, SAND, being half-starved and half-DEAD from dehydration don't lend themselves to arousal. And Bastian was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[cutting down small trees with a pocket knife? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[bodies don't burn without a shit-ton of fuel <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br /><br />And the overall plot didn't fit together - though I totally get that there's a second part.<br /><br />I know, I know, you're going to say that I've missed the point of the story . . . Sebastian Stark himself. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>You could stab me, shoot me, beat me beyond recognition - I could cope with that kind of pain. You couldn't make me feel for you - couldn't make me care because caring meant hurting in a way that I couldn't handle.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> And I would have LOVED him even more if the author had made his backstory less OTT. I felt like every detail of Bastian's past was pushed too far into the realm of improbable in order to very deliberately yank at my heartstrings.<br /><br />I'll leave you on the high note that is Bastian though. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I like the way you look at me," I said seriously. "Sometimes when you do, your eyes light up, and I think maybe I could be lucky enough for you to care about a fucked up asshole like me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Happy reading!</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer635305622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11752838144925979350"><b>4.5 Save Me, Bastian Stars!!</b><br/><br/>Gosh, where to start with this.....I FREAKING LOVED THIS BOOK! Bastian can save me from drowning, dehydration and starvation any time he wants! <br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391991801i/8484805.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Sebastian has had a tough life. Right now he just wants to enjoy his retirement on his boat hauling around rich society snobs, drinking his vodka and enjoying the occasional whore. Things were going well until a storm capsized his boat and he is left in a life raft with one other person, Raine, whom he saved from drowning.<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391991802i/8484806._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Rain</span>
  <span id="freeText11752838144925979350" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Save Me, Bastian Stars!!</b><br><br>Gosh, where to start with this.....I FREAKING LOVED THIS BOOK! Bastian can save me from drowning, dehydration and starvation any time he wants! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391991801i/8484805.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Sebastian has had a tough life. Things were going well until a storm capsized his boat and he is left in a life raft with one other person, Raine, whom he saved from drowning.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391991802i/8484806._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Raine just wanted a relaxing vacation. Life lately hasn't been easy on her either. She needs some time to regroup before going back to college. She didn't expect to have to be rescued by the ship's surly and grumpy captain. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391991802i/8484807._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Bastian is an alcoholic and along with all of their other troubles, is going through detox, which makes him even more of a prick. Raine is able to break through some of his barriers, only to discover that their pasts are intertwined. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Your…acceptance of me,” I said. “That’s really my favorite thing about you. I don’t know why you put up with my shit, but I’m glad you do."</i>
</b> ~Bastian<br><br><br>He doesn't trust easily. but somehow being with Raine has become everything to him. He knows as long as he has her, even though he thinks he doesn't deserve her, he can get through his nightly nightmares and the past the continually haunts him. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I give you my life, my love, my soul,” I swore to her. “As long as I’m breathing, I’m yours."</i>
</b> ~Bastian<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391991802i/8484808.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

  <b>5 solid stars</b>

To help save him? Well Raine does it beautifully. There was not a single moment where I thought "Oh that shouldn't have happened" or "I wanna slap her/him". The book portrays the growing relationship between two people,all in Bastian POV, (we don't really get to see how Raine thinks but her actions alone speak volumes) and it was written quite beautifully. The book does not end in a cliffhanger regarding Bastian and Raine but other problems emerge (spoilers sweetie) and I'm guessing that's what the next book covers. <br><br>This book was utterly captivating, a definite must-read. <div id="review_696880291" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/696880291" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/696880291?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=broken-hero">broken-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=hells-yeah-alphas">hells-yeah-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=jackass-heroes">jackass-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=love-hate-relationship">love-hate-relationship</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696880291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1019924506428270549"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 5 'I LOVED IT' STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385099353ra/7065498.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“Don’t touch me,” I clarified. <br/><br/>“Why not?” <br/><br/>"Because I want it and I don’t deserve it.” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I freaking loved this book. From start to finish, I could not put it down. I don't know why it took me so long to read this but I'm so glad that I finally did.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385099031i/7065438._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“Your…acceptance of me,” I said. “That’s really my </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1019924506428270549" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 5 'I LOVED IT' STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385099353ra/7065498.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Don’t touch me,” I clarified. <br><br>“Why not?” <br><br>"Because I want it and I don’t deserve it.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I freaking loved this book. From start to finish, I could not put it down. I don't know why it took me so long to read this but I'm so glad that I finally did.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385099031i/7065438._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Your…acceptance of me,” I said. “That’s really my favorite thing about you. I don’t know why you put up with my shit, but I’m glad you do.”<br><br>"You aren't that hard to accept, Bastian."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>Sebastian Stark, a.k.a. 'Daniel' is the captain of <i>The Oblivion</i>, a vacation ship for the rich that sails the Caribbean seas. Bastian is a complete and utter jackass. When he isn't sailing, he spends his time drinking booze, sleeping with whores, and smoking cigarrettes. He just plainly doesn't give a crap about anything and loves being alone. On one trip, he notices a female passenger that is by herself reading a book. He usually doesn't notice his passengers nor does he interact with them. But for some reason he notices her. After, the ship is in a wreck, he awakes to a ship in ruins and the only way to survive is to get on the raft that was left behind. When he gets on the raft, he sees someone in the water, it the female passenger he noticed before. He goes after her and saves her life. This is when they spend many weeks on a raft trying to survive.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I'll never give up," I told her. "I'll fight for you, no matter what. I don't deserve you...I'll never believe that...but I want you so bad...I need to be with you. I just have to be, Raine...I don't think I could live any other way anymore."<br><br>"Bastian," she whispered, "I'll always love you, and there's nothing that can change that."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I've got to say, I did not like Bastian one bit in the beginning. He was such a jerk that he would piss me off. And he was so crude, the things he said to poor Raine. I was SO freaking glad that this whole book was in his POV, otherwise, I wouldn't have gotten him. At. All. Bastian is hiding behind this mask so he doesn't show how hurt he is by his past, which I've got to say is really painful. I felt bad for the child and youth he was, even for the man that once loved. My heart broke for him. Soon, I inevitably fell in love with Bastian. He was so much more than he first appeared. He had a heart, he just needed to take the risk to put it out there again and let himself feel. I loved the way he later came to treat Raine. He was a total Alpha when it came to her. He was very protective, and caring. Seriously, loved him and his dirty mouth. But he also did frustrate me at times with his temper outburts. I am so happy that Bastian had Raine to help him with his demons, one being alcoholism. He wasn't perfect, but he definitely improved and became a better person towards the end.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385099031i/7065439._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I knew she wanted me. I knew she loved me. The single, brightest point in the universe wanted and loved </i>me."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Raine Gayle is a young woman trying to move on from her devastating past. Her friend tells her to vacation on this ship for a while so she can relax a bit after all the problems she has had. She never thought she would end up getting stranded with the grouchy and rude Captain. The total opposite of what she is like. He saves her time and time again. He teaches her vital things that can be a matter of life and death. She doesn't know what would have happened to her without him. As time goes by, she wants to know more about Bastian, even if it annoys the hell out him. She knows he is a kind person, despite how he likes to portray himself. She knows there is something good in him, and she helps him bring it all out. She also loves him, despite all of his flaws.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Tell me you got me," I heard her whisper through her cries.<br><br>"I've got you, Raine," I said. "I've got you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Even though, we didn't get Raine's POV, I feel like I got to know her well and was even at times able to connect with her. I think the author did a great job in being able to do that. Raine was strong and I absolutely LOVED that she didn't let Bastian stomp all over her. She was really caring, affectionate, and understanding. She somehow managed to get Bastian to open up to her. It was really lovely to read how she slowly broke down that fortress that Bastian had erected around himself. Once she bulldozed it, they were so sweet together, I love it! There were times where she didn't know things about survival, but I wouldn't call her stupid at all. She was actually quite wise at times. I just loved the fact that she never gave up on Bastian, which was exactly what he needed.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445493382ra/16661198.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You saved me in another way." I looked into her eyes, wanting her to understand what I meant so much. "You gave me something...no </i>someone<i>...to live for. There was no reason for my existence before you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b>
</blockquote><br>The sexual tension in this book was quite high in the beginning. Bastian was confused by how much he was attracted to her when he didn't even like her. Then as he got to know her, he wanted more than to just sleep with her. He craved her touches and their random talks. There were many steamy moments, I couldn't believe how HOT Bastian was. I loved the dirty things he would say and how he took care of Raine. What I enjoyed about this book, was how Bastian was able to trust again. And how the love between them developed. I couldn't get enough of them, once I started, I kept turning the page. When the ending finally came, I didn't want it to end, I wanted more. Everything is resolved and there was no cliffhanger involving their relationship, but there seems to be somethings in the past that might threaten them in the future. I CAN'T wait for the next book to come out. I seriously hope that it stays in Bastian's POV as well. I really loved this book and I would recommend everyone to give this a read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="1019924506428270549" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_601789371" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/601789371" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz"><img alt="Elizabeth (Liz)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551206872p2/5495317.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/601789371?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=ebook-read">ebook-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=5-star-reads">5-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=contemporary-romance-read">contemporary-romance-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=arc-from-author-read">arc-from-author-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer601789371" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12808747477017248311">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><br/>5 Stars<br/><br/>Shay Savage's website almost cockily proclaims that she writes "Fiction with Teeth". HA! Nothing cocky about the truth, my friends. I guarantee, that is maybe the *only* accurate way to sum up the dark, unsettling, exciting, unapologetic, fascinating, shocking, frank, graphic, primal, crude, sexy, at times horrific, consistently compelling experience that is Surviving Raine!!<br/><br/>Truly, there is just no adequate way to summarize this story. There may not </span>
  <span id="freeText12808747477017248311" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><br />5 Stars<br /><br />Shay Savage's website almost cockily proclaims that she writes "Fiction with Teeth". HA! Nothing cocky about the truth, my friends. I guarantee, that is maybe the *only* accurate way to sum up the dark, unsettling, exciting, unapologetic, fascinating, shocking, frank, graphic, primal, crude, sexy, at times horrific, consistently compelling experience that is Surviving Raine!!<br /><br />Truly, there is just no adequate way to summarize this story. There may not even be any way to review this book and do it any kind of justice. Attempting to convey just what Surviving Raine is and does and makes you feel? No, really. I don't believe it's possible. If that's a cop-out, then it's a cop-out, but it would take a far better reviewer than myself to be able to express....this....bizarre, violent, emotional, sexy mess of a story.<br /><br /><br />Here's the official blurb:<br /><br /><i>As the captain of a schooner catering to the elite on the Caribbean Seas, Sebastian Stark does his best to avoid any human encounters. Interacting with people isn’t his thing, and he prefers the company of a bottle of vodka, a shot glass, and maybe a whore. There’s no doubt he’s hiding from a checkered past, but he does well keeping everything to himself…</i><br /><br /><i>…until the night his schooner capsizes, and he’s stuck on a life raft with one of the passengers.</i><br /><br /><i>Raine’s young, she’s cute, and Bastian would probably be into her if he wasn’t suffering from alcohol withdrawal. As the days pass, DTs, starvation, and dehydration become the norm. Even the most closed person starts to open up when he thinks he’s going to die, but when she realizes their traumatic pasts are connected, it’s no longer the elements that have Bastian concerned.</i><br /><br /><i>He has no idea how he’s going to Survive Raine.</i><br /><br /><br />Sebastian is....indescribable. I know what you're thinking. You write reviews on a daily basis. Can you not do ANY BETTER THAN THIS?! But, how do you describe a character that is so horrifying one minute and so loving the next? In the real world, and even in this fictional world, I would call him mentally ill. This man is ALL. OVER. THE. MAP. He needs therapy. He needs medication. He probably needs a prison sentence. He may even need a psychiatric ward. Here's the real kicker. I found him fantastically compelling and absolutely mesmerizing. Yeah. I may need a room in that psychiatric ward right next to Sebastian Stark! <br /><br />Then there's poor, innocent, slightly stupid Raine. Well, that may not be fair. She's very young. And Sebastian is....maybe more than a little bit of a psychopath. She puts up with A LOT from him. She begins to feel she understands him and where his behavior originates from. She believes there is something worth loving in the man. There were times when I wouldn't have disagreed with her.<br /><br />Anyone who can write a story like this and elicit the kinds of reactions I've had, and continue to have, has serious talent. I don't even know where the idea for a story like this comes from. I sure as sheep don't know where a character like Sebastian Stark comes from! But, what I do know is that there are very few authors I'm aware of who could have written Surviving Raine. Scary talent. As in, YOU SCARE ME....and you're talented, too ;-)<br /><br />If this story is “Fiction with Teeth”, then those teeth sunk deep into my gut, my head, my heart, my soul. They grabbed on with everything they had and didn't once let go! Surviving Raine will shake you up, toss you around, play with your insides, and then convince you that you MUST HAVE MORE!!<br /><br />I know for a fact I can't be the only person out there who has been and will be blown away by Shay Savage and her scary talent. All my dark, gritty, twisty story lovers? Step up, sit down, and READ! This one's for you, with love, from Shay Savage. <br /><br /><br /><br />**ARC provided by author/publicist in exchange for an honest review**</span>
  <a data-text-id="12808747477017248311" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer14358208476432599195"><b>Shay Savage does it again - a story of love and redemption from the most unlikely of souls...</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403056977i/10030240._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m a heel, Raine,” I told her. “You’re my beautiful violet, and I’m always crushing you. You take away my nightmares, and I probably add to yours . I don’t think I will ever believe I deserve you, but I love you more than I can even describe. I don’t know if I can ever… be better for you, but if you’re willing to keep forgiving me for being a complete idiot, I’m willing to keep trying.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Th</span>
  <span id="freeText14358208476432599195" style="display:none"><b>Shay Savage does it again - a story of love and redemption from the most unlikely of souls...</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403056977i/10030240._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m a heel, Raine,” I told her. “You’re my beautiful violet, and I’m always crushing you. You take away my nightmares, and I probably add to yours . I don’t think I will ever believe I deserve you, but I love you more than I can even describe. I don’t know if I can ever… be better for you, but if you’re willing to keep forgiving me for being a complete idiot, I’m willing to keep trying.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> This was romantic suspense at it's best - <br><i>shipwrecks, <br>detoxing,<br>dehydration,<br>starvation,<br>desperation,<br>lost at sea...</i><br><br>When you're pretty sure there's no way you could survive, you start confessing your sins...<br><br><b>Sebastian Stark</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403185443ra/10054684.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I had never run from anything in my life. What was it about this miniscule little girl that scared the shit out of me? Once she understood everything, she was going to hate me, and the thought was extremely unnerving. I didn’t want her to hate me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Let's be honest, Bastian is an asshole... His dark and sordid past includes violence and death - just knowing the details could get Raine killed... But they're castaways, who is she going to tell? Besides, there's something about the beautiful young girl which sirs something inside Bastian...<br><br><b>Raine Gayle</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/627658.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"...I've seen you, Bastian – the real you. I know what's inside that thick skin you try to use as a shield. I've seen you at your worst, and I'm pretty sure I saw you at your best just a few minutes ago. If not then, it was when you told me not to be scared. You can't fool me anymore, Bastian. I know too much. I know you've been hurt, and I know you're scared."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Raine was hiding from the darkness of her own past... Taking a cruise on Bastian's ship before the storm came. He pulled her out of the water and saved her life. Now she must face all of the challenges of survival AND deal with Bastian's sparkling personality.<br><br>The harder Bastian tries to push Raine away, the more she gets under his skin... As the sordid details of Bastian's life come to light, the pair will discover that their histories are connected by one gruesome night...<br><br><b>A story of survival, forgiveness, acceptance, and love...</b><br><br>Perhaps you're asking yourself if you should read this book?<br>I'll let asshole Bastian answer that for you: <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Are you fucking serious?” I asked her. “Have you ever heard the phrase ‘there aren't any stupid questions?’”<br>“Yes.”<br>“Well, there are. That was one of them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Right, you heard the man! I guess you better read the book!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396625918ra/9162121.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Some of My Favorite Moments</u>
</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>It almost made life bearable. Throw in a couple of women and a bottle of something strong, and suddenly all was good in the world.<br><br>I wasn’t a people person, and one thing I tried not to do was to associate with any of the passengers <i>at all</i>. If I could avoid even seeing them, that made for the perfect trip.<br><br>I was used to death match. Last man standing. Every man for himself. You didn’t help anyone else because everyone else was going to stab you in the back the first chance they got. The primitive part of my brain kept telling me to chuck her overboard because her survival might cost me my own.<br><br>“Are you fucking serious?” I asked her. “Have you ever heard the phrase ‘there aren't any stupid questions?’”<br>“Yes.”<br>“Well, there are. That was one of them.”<br><br>“It’s a ship. Or it was. Boats are small, and size fucking matters.”<br><br>How the fuck was I going to survive with this annoying, smoking hot bitch that I simultaneously wanted to fuck and kill?<br><br>Damn, if she wasn’t going to be the death of me. I was pretty confident I could survive in a life raft for quite some time, but survive Raine without my cock jumping straight out of my shorts like a divining rod? Not so sure.<br><br>“I’m going to kiss you.”<br>“Why?” Raine’s voice was breathy and strained.<br>“I want you to get acclimated to having my lips on you,”<br><br>I was rocking back and forth again and seriously doubting whether or not I should be saying any of this to her. I also knew our chances of survival were going down really, really quickly. Maybe I needed to tell this shit to someone before I actually died.<br><br>I had never run from anything in my life. What was it about this miniscule little girl that scared the shit out of me? Once she understood everything, she was going to hate me, and the thought was extremely unnerving. I didn’t want her to hate me.<br><br>“Raine, I couldn’t save your father, but no matter what we run into, no matter how long we’re out here, no matter what God or Satan or whoever the fuck else throws at us, <i>I’m going to save you.”<br>I guess I didn’t need all that apathy after all.<br><br>"...I've seen you, Bastian – the real you. I know what's inside that thick skin you try to use as a shield. I've seen you at your worst, and I'm pretty sure I saw you at your best just a few minutes ago. If not then, it was when you told me not to be scared. You can't fool me anymore, Bastian. I know too much. I know you've been hurt, and I know you're scared."<br><br>Another tear fell down her cheek.<br>“Don’t cry, Raine. Not for me.”<br>“Someone should,” she said.<br><br>I was a brutal, inebriated killer and nothing more. I should end up alone – it was fitting and just.<br><br>I was here to save her and to love her.<br><br>“I didn’t even make you come,” I interrupted. “I used you.”<br>“You needed me,” Raine corrected, her hand on the side of my face again, turning me so I had to face her. “That’s not the same thing.”<br>“I took from you.”<br>“I gave to you.”<br>“Bullshit.”<br><br>“I’d die without you, Bastian. Even if I lived, I’d die inside.”<br><br>“Vulgar?” I mocked surprise, placing my hand over my chest. “You’re implying my speech might include vulgarities? You fucking take that shit back right now!”<br><br>Bastian Stark, asshole extraordinaire, decided to make an appearance and brought his shouty voice along with him.<br><br>“I want to make love to you,” I repeated, and because ultimately I am still an asshole, I added, “with my big…hard… cock.”<br>[...]<br>“No matter what actual words come out of my mouth – every time I think of you, every time I touch you, and every time I speak to you – I am making love to you.”<br><br>“When you look at me like that,” I said softly, “it’s like I’m looking at your soul, and you’re looking into mine. You make me feel like I’m worth something when you look at me like that.”<br><br>“I’ll always be yours ,” I told her. “No matter how much of an ass I am, you know that, don’t you? You know even when I’m being a fucked up asshole, I still love you, right?”<br><br>I had told Raine way too much, and I was pretty sure I had only told her because I hadn’t expected us to survive. She was in danger now, too.<br></i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText17410471689625857487" style="display:none">*****FOUR I WANT A BASTIAN OF MY OWN STARS!!!*****<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/3486f824989ff315c554388ec36a77ce_zps25435e14.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Bastian Stark, is the Captain of a ship called "The Oblation".<br>Raine Gayle, is a beautiful young woman, who is one of his passengers.<br>Her best friend had convinced her to take a nice vacation with some money she came into from her father's death. He was murdered in the line of duty by a crime lord.<br><br><br>During this charter, there is an earthquake, which causes the ship to capsize.<br>Bastian and Raine end up the only two on one of the rafts from the ship.<br>And so begins the first 54% of the most BORING part of this story!!!!<br>Bastian should have been named <b>BASTARD</b> during this portion of the book. He was such a complete <b>DOUCHE</b>!!<br>I get that he was going through detox, since he was an alcoholic and being that his ship was now beneath the sea, he didn't have access to any alcohol, but he was pretty tough to take!!<br>Raine was a saint for putting up with his bullshit.<br><br><br>I really wish that we hadn't spent more than half of the story on that raft, adrift at sea.<br>Maybe if just four chapters had been dedicated to the two on the raft, I would have rated this book a SOLID FIVE stars, but I had to deduct a star for making me bored to tears for two nights in a row!!!!<br><br><br>This is me during the first 54%...<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/sleeepy_zps6b8dcafe.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>I was promised by Melissa, that once we got to the island, the HOT SEX would commence and Bastian would have me swooning!!<br>So when Bastian sees land ahead, this was me...<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/minion_zps31acd39a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403235145ra/10062452.gif" alt=" photo minion_zps31acd39a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Holy Hell was Melissa right!!!!<br>I <b>LOVED LOVED LOVED</b> the second half of the book.<br>Oh how I loved Bastian and his overactive Libido and caveman ways!<br>I was comparing him to "EHD" from "Transcendence" a lot!<br>Bastian and Raine seemed to be the modern day Ehd and Beh.<br>Things heat up rather quickly between them once they are settled on the island, and Bastian is also very scared of his feelings for Raine.<br>He's not had the best childhood and had his heart broken by one woman. <br>Bastian has gone through life, in recent years, getting drunk and having plenty of sex with prostitutes.<br>He starts to have deep feelings for Raine.<br>She is "HIS", and all he wants to do is provide for her, protect her, AND "MAKE LOVE" to her!<br>Oh my GOD, this man was <b>INSATIABLE</b>!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/a01da5df3cd7ba8078ed80c280ac82ad_zps77d7fc3c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403235145i/10062453._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo a01da5df3cd7ba8078ed80c280ac82ad_zps77d7fc3c.jpg" width="375" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>There is some action during the story, which will have your heart pounding and you'll feel on edge. Bastian totally <b>KICKS ASS</b> here. This is the kind of man a woman needs to feel safe and loved!<br>However, he also has very little self worth.<br>He struggles with Raine's feelings for him. He doesn't believe he is worthy of her and tortures himself with thoughts of how she will leave him once they are rescued and back in civilization.<br>He tries being a douche to push Raine away, but she's such a kick ass heroine, that she doesn't fall for his act.<br>She definitely deserved a medal for putting up with his crap.<br>I swear he had PMS mood swings!!!<br>Eventually it does sink in his thick skull, that Raine truly does love him.<br><br><br><b>I had no purpose before her, no life, no reason to be - only existence in an empty, meaningless shell. I was useless, pointless, inadequate...the list goes on. I hated myself then, and I still did. The difference was that I knew she wanted me. I knew she loved me. The single, brightest point in the universe wanted and loved</b> <i>
  <b>me</b>
</i>.<br><br><br>Towards the end my heart broke for Bastian.<br>He was letting his insecurities get the best of him.<br>This man needs <b>A LOT</b> of love and reassurance and Raine seems to be the woman who just might be able to give that to him.<br>If she's not, I'm willing to step in her place!!! <br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17410471689625857487" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_624149936" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/624149936" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/624149936?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer624149936" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17039713191209978233"><b>4 Stormy Stars</b><br/><br/>I’ve been Surviving Raine on the back burner for a while. I think it’s because of the plot. Two people stranded by sea? But you know what?! It worked for me. My only complaint is that it was a tad bit too long, but other than that, I was swept away by this one.<br/><br/><b>Summary</b><br/><br/>Sebastian Stark is captain of a ship that gets caught up in a storm. Everyone is tossed overboard and before he finds himself a life raft, he saves a beautiful woman. Together they must endure the sea before they can g</span>
  <span id="freeText17039713191209978233" style="display:none"><b>4 Stormy Stars</b><br><br>I’ve been Surviving Raine on the back burner for a while. I think it’s because of the plot. Two people stranded by sea? But you know what?! It worked for me. My only complaint is that it was a tad bit too long, but other than that, I was swept away by this one.<br><br><b>Summary</b><br><br>Sebastian Stark is captain of a ship that gets caught up in a storm. Everyone is tossed overboard and before he finds himself a life raft, he saves a beautiful woman. Together they must endure the sea before they can get rescued.<br><br><b>Sebastian</b><br><br>Sebastian is the star of the show. I would say, this is basically his book. He’s a complex man and I wouldn’t have him any other way. You will hate him and love him at the same time. I would describe him as someone very passionate. He’s a passionate jerk and a passionate lover.<br><br><b>Riane</b><br><br>Raine is beautiful, young and not a typical girl. She’s very smart, opinionated and level headed. I loved that she isn’t your typical damsel in distress. She is kind of the perfect counterpart to Sebastian. I also like how she doesn’t put up with Sebastian’s crap.<br><br><b>Overall</b><br><br>So they are both stranded by sea and you would think the story drags but it doesn’t! Sebastian is an alcoholic and he detox and it’s so juicy to read. Sebastian teaches a lot of things to Raine and both try to survive. <br><br>Towards the middle, the relationship between Sebastian and Raine go deeper and we get a little back story to who Sebastain is and it’s pretty dramatic and dark. I loved reading it. It really explains his actions.<br><br>Surviving Raine will keep you on your toes and always question what’s going to happen next. If you want something a little different and a little tragic and a little dark, then this one is for you.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17447588.Surviving_Raine__Surviving_Raine___1_" title="Surviving Raine (Surviving Raine, #1) by Shay Savage" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1367074353s/17447588.jpg" alt="Surviving Raine (Surviving Raine, #1) by Shay Savage" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CWG930S/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00CWG930S&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=CWCU3NFLOLD6W2XW" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17039713191209978233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>
