        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer604051586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2546514390470868448"><b>4.5 Stranded Stars!!!</b><br/><br/>So I've just gotta say how much I enjoyed reading this! <br/><br/>Bastian and Raine are forced to help each other survive when Bastian's ship is wrecked by a storm. When Bastian sees Raine's body floating in the ocean, he feels an inexplicable tug, he has to save her even though he isn't even sure if she's alive. <br/><br/>He doesn't understand why he feels the way he does and because of this, he at first pushes Raine away. Acting like a complete jerk so that she doesn't become attached to him.</span>
  <span id="freeText2546514390470868448" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stranded Stars!!!</b><br><br>So I've just gotta say how much I enjoyed reading this! <br><br>Bastian and Raine are forced to help each other survive when Bastian's ship is wrecked by a storm. When Bastian sees Raine's body floating in the ocean, he feels an inexplicable tug, he has to save her even though he isn't even sure if she's alive. <br><br>He doesn't understand why he feels the way he does and because of this, he at first pushes Raine away. Acting like a complete jerk so that she doesn't become attached to him.<br><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419686i/832366._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although she's nine years younger than him, Raine isn't completely naive and she begins to chip away at the shield he's built around himself, trying to understand the man underneath.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419686i/832367.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their relationship is one shrouded in lust but at the core are two broken people who have lost so much in their lives. By being together they begin to heal each other. Bastian fights it all the way trying to brush off what they have as just being superficial. But he can't deny himself forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419686i/832368.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419686i/832369._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419686i/832370.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once again I loved it! Can't wait for the next one!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419686ra/832371.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The End...</b><br></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer622272729" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15943877525311310982"><b>
  <i>"If you call forth what is in you, it will save you. If you do not call forth what is in you, it will destroy you."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Oh, <b>WOW!</b> This book was unexpectedly great! I wasn't too sure if I would like this one when I picked it up, but boy, am I glad I took a chance and read it. This book was heartbreaking, full of tragedy and loss. It was also full of forgiveness, redemption, love, and learning one's self-worth. There were many steamy scenes to get your blood flowing and enough drama to keep you on e</span>
  <span id="freeText15943877525311310982" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"If you call forth what is in you, it will save you. If you do not call forth what is in you, it will destroy you."</i>
</b><br><br>Oh, <b>WOW!</b> This book was unexpectedly great! I wasn't too sure if I would like this one when I picked it up, but boy, am I glad I took a chance and read it. This book was heartbreaking, full of tragedy and loss. It was also full of forgiveness, redemption, love, and learning one's self-worth. There were many steamy scenes to get your blood flowing and enough drama to keep you on edge. I absolutely loved Surviving Raine! Throughout the book I came to love and adore Bastian. <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422586i/841067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> He is such a tortured soul who at his core just wants to be loved and to love in return. Raine is an amazing woman who loves unconditionally. <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422586i/841068.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> They are great for each other.<br><br><b>
  <i>"So long as men can breathe, or eyes can see, So long lives this, and this gives life to thee."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"You got me?" "Yeah, I got you."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I'll always keep you safe, I told her." "I know."</i>
</b><br><br>I cannot wait until the next book! I have found a new favorite author in Shay Savage. Read this one! <b>LOVE IT!!!!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I wanted to be with her, next to her, under her, on top of her, beside her, insider her - I wanted everything with her."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"You gave me something... no, someone... to live for. There was no reason for my existence before you."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I love you because you are worthy of my love."</i>
</b><br><br></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-m-broken">i-m-broken</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=thumbs-up-leading-lady">thumbs-up-leading-lady</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer602862356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7623665655175724511"><b>***4.25 Stars***</b><br/><br/>I've had this book on my kindle forever and if it wasn't for my traveling book club, I'm not sure when I would have gotten around to reading it....and I'm so glad I finally did! This was really good. <br/><br/>I'm a huge sucker for the bitter and damaged hero who finds hope and love because of the honest love of a woman. <br/><br/>Bastian has lived a dark and grim life so his first line of defense is a tough offense. He was an asshole through and through, but as you got to know him, his snark and an</span>
  <span id="freeText7623665655175724511" style="display:none"><b>***4.25 Stars***</b><br /><br />I've had this book on my kindle forever and if it wasn't for my traveling book club, I'm not sure when I would have gotten around to reading it....and I'm so glad I finally did! This was really good. <br /><br />I'm a huge sucker for the bitter and damaged hero who finds hope and love because of the honest love of a woman. <br /><br />Bastian has lived a dark and grim life so his first line of defense is a tough offense. He was an asshole through and through, but as you got to know him, his snark and anger made sense. <br /><br />I absolutely loved Raine. For 20 years old, she was pretty on top of her shit. She knew when to push, when to retreat and when to listen without interrupting. Such a great heroine! <br /><br />Shay Savage does a great job of writing from the male POV. It sounds authentic...not how a woman thinks a man should sound or how she thinks a man thinks....if that makes sense.</span>

          </span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('stz0RFFYscTraosHG9bNKdpn+qok9lwYTGVb5hkoA8JwB96NAQ/TTukG7CRnj0SXTfp0tTEgR/aN3VgBuow4ag==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8C6OR3slYw98n87402g2w0QMS1uVhInHEJnJYh/RrPsy9aSOK3IBhX7zqduvMb9905HFRIBSkinRIcqFvHWXUw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13019221286674087357">Shay Savage is an independent author from Cincinnati, Ohio, where she lives with her family and a variety of household pets. She is an accomplished public speaker and holds the rank of Distinguished Toastmaster from Toastmasters International. Her hobbies include off-roading in her big, yellow Jeep, science fiction in all forms, and soccer. Savage holds a degree in psychology, and she brings a lot</span>
  <span id="freeText13019221286674087357" style="display:none">Shay Savage is an independent author from Cincinnati, Ohio, where she lives with her family and a variety of household pets. She is an accomplished public speaker and holds the rank of Distinguished Toastmaster from Toastmasters International. Her hobbies include off-roading in her big, yellow Jeep, science fiction in all forms, and soccer. Savage holds a degree in psychology, and she brings a lot of that knowledge into the characters within her stories.<br /><br />From the author: “It’s my job to make you FEEL. That doesn’t always mean you’ll feel good, but I want my readers to be connected enough to my characters to care.”<br /><br />Savage’s books many books span a wide variety of topics and sub-genres with deeply flawed characters. From cavemen to addicts to hitmen, you’ll find yourself falling for these seemingly irredeemable characters!<br /><br /></span>

Available only on Amazon!  Surviving Raine Summary:  As the captain of a schooner catering to the elite on the Caribbean Seas, Sebastian Stark does his best to avoid any human encounters. Interacting with people isn’t his thing, and he prefers the company of a bottle of vodka, a shot glass, and maybe a whore. There’s no doubt he’s hiding from a checkered past, but he does well keeping everything to himself…  …until the night his schooner capsizes, and he’s stuck on a life raft with one of the passengers.  Raine’s young, she’s cute, and Bastian would probably be into her if he wasn’t suffering from alcohol withdrawal. As the days pass, DTs, starvation, and dehydration become the norm. Even the most closed person starts to open up when he thinks he’s going to die, but when she realizes their traumatic pasts are connected, it’s no longer the elements that have Bastian concerned.  He has no idea how he’s going to Survive Raine.  Bastian’s Storm – Summary  Sebastian Stark just isn’t cut out for normal life with a girlfriend in the hot and humid city of Miami. All in all, he’d rather be back on the island where it was just the two of them, and he could keep everything in balance. The bar down the street tempts him daily, but he’s determined to remain strong. Adjusting to normal life is difficult, but Bastian is doing his best to keep himself together and the nightmares away. Raine’s happy, and that’s what matters to him the most.  But not all nightmares can be driven away.  When Bastian’s former mentor comes into the picture and presents him with an ultimatum, Bastian slips into old habits. Though he wants to shield Raine from the truth, the shady circumstances of his past form into a hurricane he can’t control. In an effort to protect her, Bastian has no choice but to throw himself back into his old job – death match tournaments – just one last time.  Dropped into the arctic wilderness with weapons loaded, Bastian has to compete against representatives from major crime lords all over the states. He’s studied his competition, he knows their weaknesses, and he’s ready to battle for the woman he loves. There’s only one opponent in the mix that causes him any concern. In order to guarantee Raine’s safety, Bastian will be pitted against the key hit man for Chicago’s largest mob family – a guy who’s known as one hell of a shot.
